<h2><a name="bookmark10"></a><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;"><a name="bookmark11"></a>B</span><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">e</span><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;">n</span><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">t</span><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;">uk Perkaw</span><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">inan</span><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;"> </span><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">Yos Em</span><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">ban</span><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;font-style:italic;">g</span><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;"> di D</span><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">esa</span><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;"> Ped</span><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;text-decoration:underline;">a</span><span class="font3" style="font-weight:bold;">wa</span></h2>

<p><span class="font3">a. &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Asal-usu</span><span class="font3" style="text-decoration:underline;">l</span><span class="font3"> </span><span class="font3" style="font-style:italic;">M</span><span class="font3" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">el</span><span class="font3" style="font-style:italic;">aib Mebase T</span><span class="font3" style="font-style:italic;text-decoration:underline;">e</span><span class="font3" style="font-style:italic;">geh</span></p></li></ul>
